GSK988TA Lathe CNC System Installation and Debugging Manual
Dear Customers:
are honored and grateful you for choosing GSK988TA Lathe CNC system
from GSK CNC Equipment Co., Ltd.
This Manual the "Installation and Commissioning Manual" (software version:
V2.01) the GSK988TA Lathe CNC System, which details the installation and
commissioning the GSK988TA Lathe CNC System.
Please read this Manual carefully before installing and using the series products
order ensure product safety and normal and valid operation.
Safety Warnings
operation would lead accidents, and personnels
with appropriate qualifications can operating the system.
Special tip: The power supply installed (in) the chassis specially provided for the
CNC Systems manufactured our company.
Users are not allowed use this power supply for other purposes.
Otherwise, great danger will follow!
Important Notice:

--- Page 3 ---
Preface and Safety Precautions
Transport and storage
Product packing boxes shall not stacked for more than six layers
not climb, stand place heavy objects the packing boxes
not use cables connected the product drag carry the products
not collide scratch the panel and display screen
Product packing boxes shall protected from dampness, exposure the sun and
rain
Unpacking inspection
Please make sure the product you purchased after opening the package
Check whether the product damaged transit
Confirm the components are complete and damaged according the list
Please contact our company time case product model inconsistency,
missing accessories transport damage
Wiring
Participants wiring and inspection must competent professionals
The product must grounded reliably, with the grounding resistance more
than 0.1 Neutral wire shall not used the placement grounding wire
The wiring must correct and firm avoid product failure unexpected
consequences
Surge absorbing diodes must connected the product the specified direction,
otherwise the product will damaged
The product must powered off before plugging unplugging opening the
product chassis
Overhaul
Power supply must cut off before repairing replacing components
The failure must checked case short circuit overload, and can
restarted after troubleshooting
The power the product shall not frequently turned off. The interval
shall least min re-energization required after power-off
Statement
This Manual describes various contents much possible. However, due too
many possibilities involved, impossible describe all the operations that can

GSK988TA Lathe CNC System Installation and Debugging Manual
Warnings
Before programming and operating the product, you must read the Product Manual
and the Operation Instructions the machine tool manufacturer detail, and
perform related operations strict accordance with the requirements the
Manual and the Instructions; otherwise may cause damage the product and
machine tool, work piece scrapping even personal injury.
Note
The product functions and technical indicators (such accuracy, speed, etc.)
described this manual are only for this product. The actual function configuration
and technical performance CNC machine tool are determined the design the
machine tool manufacturer, which are subject the instruction manual the
machine tool manufacturer.
Please refer the Operation Instructions the machine tool manufacturer for the
function and meaning keys the machine panel.
The content this manual subject change without notice.
Safety Warnings

人 广州 GSK988TA_Lathe CNC and_Debugging Manual The electric cabinet must able effectively prevent the entry dust, coolant and organic 一 When designing the electrical cabinet, the distance between the CNC back cover and the chassis should not less than 20cm. When the temperature inside the electrical cabinet rises, The display panel must installed where the sprayed coolant unable reach. When designing the electrical cabinet, please consider reducing external electrical interference much possible prevent the interference transmitted the CNC. The following grounding system provided for CNC machine tools. Signal Ground Frame Ground System earthing 1.3.3 Methods prevent interference The CNC should far away from the equipment that causes interference (such frequency 他 supply power the CNC through the isolation transformer, the machine tool where the CNC
1.3 GSK988TA product installation solution. must ensured that the temperature difference inside and outside the cabinet does not 1.3.2 System grounding requirements The signal ground provides the reference voltage (OV) the telecommunication system. Frame grounding used for safety, and frame unit shell, panel and interface cables among each unit The system ground used connect the frame ground the equipment and the unit the ground. the design CNC, anti-interference measures such shielding electromagnetic radiation the space, converter, contactor, electrostatic generator, high voltage generator and power line segmentation installed must grounded, and the CNC and the drive unit must connected independent
1.3.1 Installation conditions electrical cabinet exceed 10°C. must connected together. The frame ground can also suppress internal and external noise. absorbing Impulse current, and filtering out power supply clutter etc. have been adopted, which can prevent device, etc.);
order ensure the internal air circulation, fan can installed the electric cabinet. the influence external interference sources the CNC itself certain extent. order ensure the
stable operation CNC, necessary take the following measures when installing and connecting the
CNC:

2.4 UseofCNC input and output Signals
The input and output Signals CNC include high-speed input and output Signals the CNC host，
special signals for band switches the machine operation panel, special signals for external keys the
operation panel, and general input and output signals the operation panel.
2.4.1 Input signal 到
i=]
The input signal refers the signal from the electrical circuit the machine tool the panel the
machine tool the CNC. When the interface input point connected +24V (Note: the band switch
dedicated interface connected +5V), the input valid, and the corresponding address signal state
When the interface input point disconnected from +24V, the input invalid, and the corresponding
address signal state The contact the input signal the machine side should meet the following
conditions:
Contact capacity: DC30V, more.
Leakage current between contacts when open circuit: ImA less.
The voltage drop between the contacts when the circuit closed: less (current 8.5mA, including the
voltage drop the cable).
There are two ways externally input the input signal: one uses contact switch input, the connection
shown Fig. 2-17.

1.1.2 Custom parameter settings
1.1.2.1 Custom parameter configuration file description
The user can integrate the required system parameters PLC parameters writing configuration file,
which convenient for the user conFig. and debug the parameters. The configuration file written
standard RGL format, the file name can defined itself, and the suffix .RGL. can written
Notepad PC. The content the configuration file mainly composed four parts: project ([project]),

--- Page 55 ---
Chapter Machine Tool Commissioning and Operation
section ([section]), and notes ([note_start], [note_end]).
Users can add more detailed notes the comment section. See for example.
[project] Paragraph
Format: [project] project name
[note start]
[note_end]

system parameter and PLC parameter setting range

1.3.5 PLC program transmission
PLC program transmission can only carried out the authority above the machine manufacturer
level (level 2).
There are two ways transfer PLC programs:
Use GSKComm-M for transmission. For detailed operations, please refer "1.7 Use
Communication Software GSKComm-M" this chapter.
Use disk transfer single PLC program the ladder diagram page, perform batch PLC
program transfer the file management page. For detailed operations, please refer "1.2 Disk
Operation" this chapter.

When the numerator the electronic gear ratio (CMR/DMR) the CNC side greater than the
denominator, the maximum speed allowed the CNC will decrease. When the numerator the electronic
gear ratio smaller than the denominator, the positioning accuracy CNC may decrease. order ensure
the positioning accuracy and speed index CNC, when supporting digital servo with electronic gear ratio
function, recommended set the electronic gear ratio CNC 1:1, and set the calculated electronic
gear ratio the digital servo.

2.6 Adjustment acceleration and deceleration
The larger the acceleration and deceleration time constant, the slower the acceleration and deceleration
process, the smaller the impact the machine tool movement, and the lower the processing efficiency; the
smaller the acceleration and deceleration time constant, the faster the acceleration and deceleration process,
and the greater the impact the machine tool movement. The higher the efficiency the time.
When the acceleration/deceleration time constant the same, the higher the start/end speed
acceleration/deceleration, the faster the acceleration/deceleration process, the greater the impact the
machine tool movement, the higher the processing efficiency; the lower the start/end speed acceleration and
deceleration, the slower the acceleration/deceleration process, the smaller the impact the machine tool
movement, and the lower the processing efficiency.
The principle acceleration/deceleration adjustment appropriately reduce the acceleration
/deceleration time constant and increase the start/stop speed acceleration and deceleration the premise
that the drive unit does not alarm, the motor does not lose step and the machine tool movement has obvious
impact, improve the processing efficiency. the acceleration/deceleration time constant set too
small, and the acceleration/deceleration start/end speed set too high, easy cause the drive unit
alarm, the motor out step, the machine tool vibration.
Setting related parameters the following situations:
Fast runtime
During fast running, the program segment
tom

Linear acceleration and deceleration S-type acceleration and deceleration

that the speed can lowered ensure accurate zero return. The faster the mechanical zero
return performed, the longer the zero return block, otherwise the moving carriage will rush
through the zero return block due CNC acceleration and deceleration, machine inertia, ete.,
and there not enough deceleration distance, which will affect the accuracy zero return.
addition, before returning zero, make sure that the carriage will not interfere with other parts
the machine tool during the zero return movement ensure safety.

When the system sets the function returning the reference point without stopper valid, the
machine tool can realize the reference point return without installing deceleration switch. When the tool
returns the reference point, the end the return reference point LED light on, and the coordinate
system automatically set.

The machine tool feeds along the axis the return direction the reference point, that stops
near the reference point, but does not exceed the reference point position.

position).

2.8.2 Double-directional pitch error compensation
The stored pitch error compensation does not distinguish the direction movement. However, the
two-way pitch error compensation, you can distinguish and set the amount pitch error compensation when
moving the positive direction and when moving the negative direction, and perform pitch error
compensation different directions. addition, when the movement reversed, the compensation amount
automatically calculated based the pitch error compensation data, and the compensation when the
movement direction reversed the same the backlash compensation. result, the path difference
between the positive direction and the negative direction can further reduced. 一
use the two-way pitch error compensation function, set the two-way pitch error compensation
function valid (parameter No.3605#0="1”).

2.10.2 Spindle speed control 二
和
所
There are two ways control the spindle speed, which can selected parameters. The first use
communication control the servo drive unit when connecting the GSK-Link spindle. The second use
the analog voltage output port the extended I/O unit output and send analog voltage 10V
the spindle servo drive device inverter. Infinitely variable speed can achieved matter which method
adopted.
Although command the spindle speed, the actual control object the spindle motor. Therefore, CNC
must have certain correspondence between the speed and grade the spindle motor. This system determines
the gear stage currently used the machine tool gear selection signals (GR1, GR2), and CNC outputs the
spindle speed corresponding the gear stage. The spindle speed control process follows:

2.12 Parallel program function
Parallel programs can run programs different from the main program the same time during automatic
operation. result, possible control the loader axis and back drill axis parallel with the main
160

--- Page 177 ---
Chapter Machine Debugging and Function
program.
The parallel program function can triggered the signal call the specified program. addition,
the parallel program can loaded the main program and then executed. auxiliary function, this
function can executed parallel with the automatic running program.
The parallel program function currently only supports G00, G01, G04, G28, G35, instructions and most
auxiliary codes.
Note Before using the parallel program function, dedicated PLC program support required.
Note Parallel program function does not support M99 instruction.
Note The motion instructions the parallel program cannot conflict with the main program being executed.

2.14.4 Additional axis acceleration/deceleration feature adjustment
The larger the acceleration/deceleration time constant, the slower the acceleration/ deceleration process,
the smaller the impact the machine tool movement, and the lower the processing efficiency; the smaller the
172

--- Page 189 ---
Chapter Machine Debugging and Function
acceleration/deceleration time constant, the faster the acceleration/ deceleration process, and the greater the
impact the machine tool movement, and the higher the efficiency the time.
When the acceleration/deceleration time constant the same, the higher the start/end speed
acceleration/deceleration, the faster the acceleration/deceleration process, the greater the impact the
machine tool movement, the higher the processing efficiency; the lower the start/end speed acceleration and
deceleration, the slower the acceleration/deceleration process, the smaller the impact the machine tool
movement, and the lower the processing efficiency.
The principle acceleration/deceleration adjustment appropriately reduce the acceleration
/deceleration time constant and increase the start/stop speed acceleration and deceleration the premise
that the drive unit does not alarm, the motor does not lose step and the machine tool movement has obvious
impact, improve the processing efficiency. the acceleration/deceleration time constant set too
small, and the acceleration/deceleration start/end speed set too high, easy cause the drive unit 三
alarm, the motor out step, the machine tool vibration.

3.3. Remote monitoring function
The GSK988TA remote monitoring function read the display information the current page the
GSK988TA CNC system through the software, and can operate the editing keyboard the monitored
system and manage the files the GSK988TA, including processing files, parameter files, tool offsets and
pitch errors Compensation files and ladder diagram files, etc.
enable the remote monitoring function, first set the parameter No.930.0 (RMEN) "1", and start the
remote monitoring server software RmServer and client software RmClient software. The connection diagram

3.4 Remote data communication function
The remote data communication function the secondary development the GSK988TA CNC system.
When the customer needs the application software the connect the GSK988TA CNC system
through the network perform online diagnosis production monitoring and management the system, the
company provides the communication that the customer needs. Protocol connection package, customers can
connect the GSK988TA CNC system loading the data communication protocol, including single
multiple systems connected form network the same time. The customer needs any information the
system, just call various communication interfaces provided the system manufacturer, including coordinate
values, number processed pieces, alarm information and various processing data.
The CNC system needs enable the remote data communication function allow external connections.
Set parameter No.930.1 (NDSVR) "I", and set the address the connected the setting
page.
3.45 MODBUS data communication function
GSK988TA CNC system provides standard MODBUS data communication protocol, which can read
most the system information. Like the remote data communication function, this function also
secondary development the GSK988TA CNC system and provided customers who need use this
protocol connect the CNC system.
The CNC system needs turn the MODBUS communication switch allow external connections.
Set parameter No.930.2 (MODBUS) "I", and set the address the connected the setting
page.
3.6 Remote servo data sampling function
GSK988TA remote servo data sampling function read the data the servo connected the current
system through software, and can analyze the collected servo data.
enable the remote monitoring function, first set the parameter No.930.3 (LABTUNE) "I" and start
the GSK CNC system debugging tool. After the network connection completed, the page displayed the
shown Fig. 3-6.

Appendix 2.2 The definition standard ladder diagram and address
The I/O GSK988TA divided into high-speed I/O signal and general I/O signal. The high-speed
signal the one the CN61 interface the back cover the CNC. The general I/O signal the one the
expansion I/O unit. The functions CNC I/O signals (except the signals marked with fixed addresses) are
defined the built-in PLC program (ladder diagram) the system. When the GSK988TA system
assembled with the machine tool, the I/O function determined the machine tool manufacturer's design.
Please refer the machine tool for details. Manufacturer’s commands.
this section, the general I/O signal (ie address) function described for the GSK988TA standard
PLC program, please pay attention!

Appendix 2.2.2 General Machine Tool I/O Interface
The general input and output GSK988TA are distributed through GSK-Link communication
connection I/O unit. maximum I/O units can connected through the GSK-Link bus, each I/O unit has
maximum input points and output points. The address range X80~X127 and Y80~Y 127, and the
user needs customize according their needs ConFig. the system address.
I/O unit with input points and output points conFig.d the standard configuration
GSK988TA. The configuration addresses the standard ladder diagram the system are X100~X105 and
100~Y 103, all which are introduced this manual I/O signal addresses are all based this standard.
